### 1208758494568910848
## RyanQ (ryanrq) 02/18/2024 12:54 

> Just as a word of warning, if anybody wants to try the Android 15 Dev Preview, DO NOT SIDELOAD THE OTA, IT WILL BRICK YOUR PHONE, FLASH THE FACTORY IMAGE INSTEAD!!!. You might be able to recover if you have an unlocked bootloader before the flash, but if you don't you'll be completely out of luck and your phone will turn into a paperweight.
> 
> After the installation is done it will fail to decrypt your Android 14 data on reboot and it won't boot. The only way to successfully install is by flashing the factory image which will wipe the data on the phone and that will work fine.
> 
> More into this: https://x.com/nexusben/status/1758602539337932995
> 
> https://x.com/TECHNIKVERBOT/status/1758614281233306033
